# Pp

# ***\*p.m.*** adv
英音 ˌpiː'em     美音 ˌpiː'em  

| 词频 4 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **午后；下午**  


# ***\*pace*** n
英音 peɪs     美音 peɪs  

| 词频 3 | 书面 1 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **[C] 一步：**  

 > Walk / Take ten paces forward.  
 > 向前走十步。  

### 2.*高义频：* **[U] [常用单数] 速度；进度：**  

 > **at a fast pace**  
 > He walked at a fast pace.   
 > 他疾步行走。  

 > **at their own pace**  
 > Students study at their own pace and the teachers seldom set tests.   
 > 学生按自己的进度学习，老师很少安排考试。  
 > 来源：北师大⑤ – 15  

 > **pace of life**  
 > pace of life  
 > 生活节奏  


固定搭配
---
## \*keep pace (with sb / sth)
1.**(与某人 / 事物) 并驾齐驱；步调一致**

---

# ***\*pack*** v
英音 pæk     美音 pæk  

| 词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 1 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **(把…) 打包；(把…) 装进 (箱子等) ：**  

 > Don’t forget to pack your toothbrush!   
 > 别忘了把牙刷放到箱子里去!  

 > I haven’t packed yet.   
 > 我还没收拾行李呢。  

 > **packed their things / belongings**  
 > They hurriedly packed their things / belongings into the suitcase.  
 > 他们匆忙地把东西装进了行李箱。  
 > 来源：2009 江西改  

### 2.*高义频：* **塞满；挤满：**  

 > More than two thousand students packed the hall.   
 > 两千多名学生把礼堂挤得满满的。  

 > **packed with**  
 > The bus was packed with people.   
 > 公共汽车上挤满了人。  

 > **packed into**  
 > We all packed into one car.  
 > 我们都挤进了一辆车里。  


固定搭配
---
## \*pack up
1.**把…打包；收拾 (行李)：**  

 > Once a friend and I packed up some peanut butter and sandwiches for an outing.   
 > 有一次，我和一个朋友包好一些花生酱和三明治去郊游。  
 > 来源：2009 浙江  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
We were first greeted with the barking by a pack ________ dogs, seven to be exact.  
##### 来源：2019 全国  
##### 答案 of  
  
##### 题目  
The workers ________ (把…打包) the glasses and marked on each box “This Side Up”.  
##### 来源：2010 全国改  
##### 答案 packed  
  

# ***\*pack*** n
英音 pæk     美音 pæk  

| 词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 1 |  

用法点拨  [C]

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **(一) 包；(一) 捆；包裹：**  

 > The horse carried two packs on its back.   
 > 那匹马背上驮着两包东西。  

### 2.*高义频：* **(商品的) 纸包；纸盒：**  

 > a food pack   
 > 食品包  

 > **pack of**  
 > a pack of cigarettes  
 > 一包香烟  

### 3.*低义频：* **背包：**  

### 4.*低义频：* **一群；一帮；一堆：**  

 > **pack of**  
 > a pack of fools / wolves  
 > 一群傻子/狼  

 > The red wolf hunts at night, alone or in small packs.  
 > 红狼夜间单独或小群捕食。

英文释义
---

 > a package of biscuits   
 > 一包饼干

 > a package tour  
 > 包价旅游 / 跟团游

 > 软件包

# ***\*pain*** n
英音 peɪn     美音 peɪn  

| 词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 |  

用法点拨  [C] & [U]

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **(肉体上的) 痛；疼痛：**  

 > **have a pain in my stomach / stomach pains**  
 > I have a pain in my stomach / stomach pains.  
 > 我胃痛。  

 > have pain all over   
 > 全身疼痛  

### 2.*高义频：* **(精神上的) 痛苦；苦恼：**  

 > **cause (sb) pain**  
 > cause (sb) pain  
 > 使某人痛苦  

 > The parents are still in great pain over the death of their child.   
 > 那对父母仍处于孩子离世带来的痛苦之中。  

 > No pain, no gain.  
 > 不劳无获。  


固定搭配
---
## \*take pains to do sth 
1.**努力 / 下苦功做某事：**  

 > We should take pains to improve ourselves through learning and get prepared for the future.  
 > 我们应该通过学习努力改善自己，并为将来作好准备。  
 > 来源：2015 福建书面表达  


派生词汇
---
painless /'peɪnləs/ adj   

# ***\*painful*** adj
英音 'peɪnfl     美音 'peɪnfl  

| 词频 4 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **令人疼痛的；引起痛苦的**  
反义词 painless 

 > **painful experience**  
 > Learning English as a second language can be a painful experience.  
 > 把英语作为第二语言来学习时一段痛苦的经历。  
 > 来源：2019 全国  

 > My legs become painful.  
 > 我的腿开始疼了。  


派生词汇
---

# ***\*pair*** n
英音 peə(r)     美音 per  

| 词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 |  

用法点拨  [C]

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **一双 / 对；一把 / 副：**  

 > The shoes are too small for me. Show me another pair.   
 > 这鞋我穿着太小，再给我拿一双看看。  

 > a pair of earrings / glasses / trousers / chopsticks   
 > 一对耳环/一副眼镜/一条裤子/一双筷子  

Notes: 一般可在pair前加定语。  
 > a new pair of shoes  
 > 一双新鞋  

 > a sharp pair of eyes  
 > 一双敏锐的眼睛  

Notes: “a pair of +复数名词”作主语时，谓语动 词通常用单数形式。  
 > A pair of gloves is a welcome present.  
 > 手套是一件受欢迎的礼物。  


固定搭配
---
## \*in pairs 
1.**成对地；两人一组地：**  

 > I want you to do this task in pairs.   
 > 我希望你们两人一组完成这项任务。

---

### 2.*高义频：* **(光线) 暗淡的；微弱的：**  

 > a pale moon   
 > 朦胧的月色  

### 3.*高义频：* **苍白的；灰白的：**  

 > **went / turned pale.**  
 > On hearing the news of the school shooting, she went / turned pale.  
 > 听到校园枪击事件的消息，她脸色苍白。  

 > He looks pale from his long illness.   
 > 他因长期生病而脸色苍白。

# ***\*panic*** n
英音 'pænɪk     美音 'pænɪk  

| 词频 3 | 口语 1 |  

用法点拨  [C] & [U]

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **恐慌；惊慌：**  

 > The news has caused panic.   
 > 这条消息已引起了恐慌。  

 > **in (a) panic**  
 > Hundreds of people left their homes in (a) panic.  
 > 上百人惊慌地离开了他们的家园。  
 > 来源：外研⑧ – 5改

---

“Tommy, run! Be quick! The house is on fire!” the mother shouted, with ________ (恐慌) clearly in her voice.  
##### 来源：2011 湖北改  
##### 答案 panic

固定搭配
---
## \*I beg your pardon
1.*高义频：* **[未听清对方的话，请求重复；常简化为 “beg pardon” 或 “pardon”] 什么；请再说一遍：**  

 > — You’re very quiet today.   
 > 你今天话很少啊。  

 > — Pardon?   
 > 什么？  

 > — I said you’re very quiet today.   
 > 我说你今天话很少。  

2.*低义频：* **[表示道歉] 对不起；请原谅：**  

 > I beg your pardon. I didn’t know this was your seat.  
 > 对不起，我不知道这座位是你的。  


# ***\*pardon*** vt
英音 'pɑːdn     美音 'pɑːrdn  

| 词频 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **[正式用语] [不用于进行时] 原谅；宽恕 (forgive)：**  

 > **Pardon,for**  
 > Pardon me for interrupting you.  
 > 对不起，打扰你了。  

 > — Can you read the sign, sir? No smoking allowed in the lift!  
 > 先生，请看一下告示牌好吗？电梯里禁止吸烟！  

 > **Pardon me**  
 > — Pardon me.  
 > 对不起。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
— Can you read the sign, sir? No smoking allowed in the lift!
— ________.   
A.Never mind   
B.Don’t mention it  
C.Sure, I don’t smoke   
D.Pardon me  
##### 来源：2007 全国  
##### 答案 D

# ***\*part*** n
英音 pɑːt     美音 pɑːrt  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

用法点拨  [C]

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **部分；一部分：**  

 > divide the cheese into three equal parts   
 > 将奶酪分成三等份  

 > **a,part of**  
 > Music has become (a) part of my life.   
 > 音乐已经成为了我生活中的一部分。  

 > **an important part of**  
 > Vocabulary is an important part of language, just like bricks in a building.   
 > 词汇是语言的重要组成部分，正如盖楼的砖一样。  
 > 来源：2010 江苏  

Notes: part前有形容词修饰时使用不定冠词，没有形容词修饰时通常不用冠词。  
### 2.*高义频：* **(机器的) 零件；(人、动植物的) 器官；部位：**  

 > **spare parts**  
 > spare parts   
 > 备用零件  

 > the parts of the body  
 > 身体各部位  

### 3.*高义频：* **[常用复数] 地区：**  

 > They try their best to find Olympic stamps issued by various parts of the world.   
 > 他们尽全力搜集世界各地发行的奥运邮票。  
 > 来源：2012 江西  

### 4.*高义频：* **角色：**  

 > **play the part of**  
 > In the play, Adam will play the part of the leading role.  
 > 在剧中，亚当将扮演主角。  


固定搭配
---
## \*for the most part 
1.**通常；多数情况下：**  

 > For the most part, students work to earn money for their own use.   
 > 大多数情况下，学生打工赚钱是为了自己用。  

## \*in part 
1.**部分地；在某种程度上：**  

 > Some people said his success was due in part to luck.  
 > 有人说他成功的部分原因是运气好。  

## \*play / act a(n) (...) part (in)
1.**(在…中) 扮演角色 / 起作用：**  

 > Nowadays, the Internet plays an important part in our lives.   
 > 如今，互联网在我们的生活中起着重要作用。  

## \*take part (in) 
1.**参加；参与：**  

 > If Jim took part in the Talent Show, he’d win it for sure.   
 > 如果吉姆参加才艺大赛，他肯定会赢。  
 > 来源：北师大② – 5  

 > Eleven million students in Jiangsu took an active part in this program.   
 > 1100万江苏学生积极参与了这个项目。  

Notes: take part in是固定搭配，part前一般不用冠词，但part前有形容词修饰时，要用不定冠词。  
#### 辨析 join, join in, take part in, attend
四者都常译为“参加”。

 > The wind parted the smoke just enough for him to catch sight of Sibson.   
 > 风吹散了浓烟，刚好让他看见了希伯森。  
 > 来源：2012 四川

# ***\*particular*** adj
英音 pə'tɪkjələ(r)     美音 pər'tɪkjələr  

| 词频 4 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **[只用于名词前] 特定的**  
英译 used to emphasize that you are talking about one person, thing, time, etc. and not about others (specific)：

 > He did not show up on that particular day.   
 > 他并没有在那一天露面。  

 > The giant panda eats only one particular type of bamboo.  
 > 大熊猫只吃某一种竹子。  

### 2.*高义频：* **特别的；格外的：**  

 > **nothing particular**  
 > I have nothing particular to do this evening.   
 > 今晚我没有什么特别的事要做。  

 > We must pay particular attention to this point.   
 > 我们必须要特别注意这一点。  

### 3.*低义频：* **讲究的；挑剔的：**  

 > a particular customer   
 > 挑剔的顾客  

 > **particular about / over**  
 > She is very particular about / over her appearance.  
 > 她很在意自己的外表。  


固定搭配
---
## \*in particular 
1.**尤其；特别：**  

 > Parents and coaches in particular should act as better examples for children.   
 > 父母和教练尤其要给孩子们树立更好的榜样。  
 > 来源：2008 上海  

 > Are you doing anything in particular this weekend?  
 > 这个周末你有什么特别的安排吗？  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
She has already tried her best. Please don’t be too particular ________ her job.   
##### 来源：2011 江西改  
##### 答案 about / over

英文释义

 > The micro blog has exploded in popularity in recent years, particularly among young people.   
 > 近年来微博大受欢迎，尤其是在年轻人当中。

# ***\*pass*** v
英音 pɑːs     美音 pæs  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **经过：**  

 > Please let me pass.   
 > 请让我过去。  

 > She passes my house on her way to school.   
 > 她上学时路过我家。  

### 2.*高义频：* **超过：**  

 > China passed the US to become the largest mobile phone market in the world.  
 > 中国超过了美国成为世界上最大的手机市场。  
 > 来源：外研① – 6  

### 3.*高义频：* **通过 (考试、议案等)：**  

 > **pass a law**  
 > pass a law   
 > 通过一项法律  

 > To reach the goal, I must first try my best to pass the College Entrance Examination and enter a good university.  
 > 为实现这一目标，我必须先尽全力通过高考，考入一所好大学。  
 > 来源：2010 湖北书面表达  

### 4.*高义频：* **度过 (时间)；(时间) 流逝：**  

 > **pass the time**  
 > We sang songs to pass the time.   
 > 我们借唱歌来消磨时间。  

 > Many years have passed, but I still remember it as if it were yesterday.   
 > 许多年过去了，但记忆中的一切仿佛就在昨天。  

### 5.*高义频：* **递；传递：**  

- pass sb sth / pass sth to sb:

 > Please pass me the book. / Please pass the book to me.  
 > 请把书递给我。  


固定搭配
---
## \*pass around / round 
1.**分发；传阅：**  

 > Pass the cookies around / round, would you?   
 > 请把小甜饼分发给大家，好吗？  

## \*pass away 
1.**[委婉语] 去世；逝世：**  

 > He unfortunately passed away last year due to his cancer.  
 > 他去年因癌症不幸去世。  
 > 来源：2015 江苏  

## \*pass by 
1.**经过；(时间) 过去：**  

 > Did you see a man in black pass by just now?   
 > 你刚才有没有看见一位身穿黑色衣服的男子经过？  

 > Three hours passing by, I became more and more impatient.   
 > 3小时过去了，我越来越不耐烦。  
 > 来源：2009 重庆  

## \*pass down 
1.**把…传下去 (hand down)：**  

 > She wants to be a gymnastics coach to pass down what she’s learned to other kids when she grows up.   
 > 她长大后想成为一名体操教练，把她所学的传授给其他孩子。  
 > 来源：2013 北京  

## \*pass off as
1.**把…冒充成：**  

 > He escaped by passing himself off as a guard.   
 > 他冒充警卫逃走了。  

## \*pass on 
1.**传递：**  

 > Please pass on the message to as many people as possible.   
 > 请将这个消息传达给尽可能多的人。  

## \*pass out 
1.**分发；分配；昏倒：**  

 > In the home for sick people, I helped wash clothes and sheets, and pass out lunch.   
 > 在患者之家，我帮忙洗衣服和床单，分发午餐。  
 > 来源：2008 四川  

 > I nearly passed out when I saw all the blood.   
 > 看到那么多血，我差点晕了过去。  

## \*pass through 
1.**穿过；通过**  

## \*pass up
1.**放弃；错过 (机会等)：**  

 > You shouldn’t pass up the opportunity to go to university.  
 > 你不该放弃上大学的机会。  


派生词汇
---
passing /'pɑːsɪŋ/ adj   
 > **passing interest**  
 > a passing interest / thought   
 > 一时的兴趣/想法

英文释义

### 1.*高义频：* **过去的；以往的；结束了的：**  

 > The club is holding a party for past and present members.   
 > 俱乐部正在为前会员和现会员举办聚会。  
 > 来源：2012 上海  

 > Winter is past and spring has come.   
 > 冬去春来。  

 > Great changes have taken place in the school over / in the past three years.  
 > 在过去三年里，这所学校发生了巨大的变化。  
 > 来源：2011 福建书面表达改  

### 2.*低义频：* **过去式的**

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 2 |  

英文释义

 > 几个月过去了，一直没有消息。

# ***\*pay*** n  重难点词汇
英音 peɪ     美音 peɪ  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

用法点拨  [U]

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **工资；薪水：**  

 > **low / high pay**  
 > low / high pay   
 > 低/高薪  

#### 辨析 pay, salary, wage
三者都可用作名词，含“报酬”之意，都常译为“工资”。  


# ***\*pay*** v  重难点词汇
英音 peɪ     美音 peɪ  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

用法点拨  (paid, paid)

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **付 (钱)；支付：**  

 > **pay a bill**  
 > pay a bill   
 > 支付账单  

 > a low-paid / well-paid job   
 > 低/高薪工作  

 > **paying in cash**  
 > — Are you paying in cash or by credit card?   
 > 你付现金还是刷信用卡?  

 > **pay cash**  
 > — I’ll pay cash.   
 > 我付现金。  

- pay sb sth:

 > I paid him 20 dollars to repair my bike.   
 > 我付给他20美元修自行车。  

- pay for sth:

 > I have to pay for the book lost.   
 > 我不得不为丢失的书支付赔偿金。  

- pay sth for sth:

 > He paid $2,000 for his new computer.   
 > 他买新电脑花了2000美金。  

- pay sb for sth:

 > Did Linda pay you for looking after her baby?   
 > 琳达付给你看孩子的钱了吗？  

#### 辨析 cost, spend, pay, take
这四个词都经常译为“花费”，但用法各不相同。  

### 2.*高义频：* **给予 (注意)；进行 (访问)：**  

 > **pay attention to**  
 > pay attention to   
 > 注意  

 > **pay a visit to**  
 > pay a visit to sb / pay sb a visit  
 > 拜访某人  


固定搭配
---
## \*pay back
1.*高义频：* **偿还；报答：**  

 > Will you lend me $10? I’ll pay (it) back next month.  
 > 你借给我10美元好吗？我下个月还你。  

 > That I can pay back the help people give me makes me happy.   
 > 能够回报人们给我的帮助让我感到很开心。  
 > 来源：译林③ – 1  

2.*高义频：* **报复：**  

 > Pay somebody back in his own coin.   
 > 以其人之道还治其人之身。  

## \*pay down
1.**先支付 (部分货款) 作为定金**  

## \*pay off
1.*低义频：* **还清 (欠债等)：**  

 > Once we’ve paid off the debts, we’ll owe money to no one.   
 > 一旦还清了债务，我们就不欠任何人的钱了。  

2.*高义频：* **取得成功；得到好结果：**  

 > He studied hard before the examination, and it paid off. He made an A.   
 > 他在考试前努力学习，功夫没有白费，他得了个A。  

3.*低义频：* **付清工资后解雇；遣散：**  

 > Over 1,000 workers will be paid off if this factory closes.   
 > 如果这家工厂关闭，会有超过1000名工人被解雇。  

## \*pay up
1.**(尤指不情愿或延迟) 付清欠款；偿还欠款**  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
— Dad, I don’t think Oliver the right sort of person for the job.

##### 来源：2014 江苏改  
##### 答案 off  
  
##### 题目  
The watch was very good, and he paid 20 percent down ________ it.  
##### 来源：2013 全国改  
##### 答案 for  
  
##### 题目  
The athlete’s years of hard training paid ________ when she finally won the Olympic gold medal.  
##### 来源：2012 安徽改  
##### 答案 off

固定搭配
---

 > 这两个社区相安无事。

 > 争吵了两周后，他们终于和好了。

# ***\*people*** n
英音 'piːpl     美音 'piːpl  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **[复数概念，谓语动词用复数形式] 人；人们：**  

 > At least ten people were killed in the crash.   
 > 至少有10人在撞车事故中丧生。  

### 2.*高义频：* **[与the连用，谓语动词用复数形式] 人民：**  

 > serve the people heart and soul   
 > 全心全意为人民服务  

 > He lived for the people and died for the people.   
 > 他为人民而生，为人民而死。  

### 3.*高义频：* **[C] (pl peoples) 民族；种族：**  

 > the peoples of Europe   
 > 欧洲各民族

# ***\*percent*** n
英音 pə'sent     美音 pə'sent  

| 词频 5 | 口语 1 | 书面 2 |  

用法点拨  [亦作per cent，单复数相同]

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **百分之...：**  

 > **one / a hundred percent**  
 > Don’t promise anything unless you are one / a hundred percent (= completely) sure.  
 > 除非你有百分之百的把握，否则不要答应任何事。  
 > 来源：2008 浙江  

Notes: “percent of + 名词 / 代词”作主语，名词 / 代词为复数时，谓语动词用复数；名词为不可数名词或代词为单数时，谓语动词用单数。  
 > Ten percent of the students are absent today.   
 > 今天有10%的学生缺席。  

 > About 30 percent of the land is covered in forest.  
 > 这片陆地约30%覆盖着森林。

---
### 1.**每一百中**

# ***\*perfect*** adj
英音 'pɜːfɪkt     美音 'pɜːrfɪkt  

| 词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **完美的；极好的**  
反义词 imperfect： 

 > He speaks perfect English.   
 > 他讲一口地道的英语。  

 > The car is in perfect condition.   
 > 车况极佳。  

 > — What do you think of the house?  
 > 这个房子怎么样？  

 > — Perfect! It’s everything we’ve been looking for.  
 > 好极了！一切都是我们想要的。  
 > 来源：2013 辽宁改  

### 2.*高义频：* **最适当的；理想的：**  

 > **perfect for**  
 > The weather was perfect for the outdoor performance.  
 > 天气很适合户外活动。  

 > **perfect for**  
 > She is perfect for the job.   
 > 她做那项工作再合适不过了。  


派生词汇
---
perfection /pə'fekʃn/ n [U]   

# ***\*perfectly*** adv
英音 'pɜːfɪktli     美音 'pɜːrfɪktli  

| 词频 3 | 口语 2 | 书面 1 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **非常；十分；完全地：**  

 > I found a dress that suited me perfectly.   
 > 我找了一件非常适合我的衣服。  
 > 来源：外研⑦ – 2  

 > — Do you understand?   
 > 你明白吗？  

 > — Perfectly.   
 > 完全明白。  


# ***\*perform*** v  重难点词汇
英音 pə'fɔːm     美音 pər'fɔːrm  

| 词频 4 | 口语 1 | 书面 2 | 阅读 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **vt履行；执行；做 (carry out)：**  

 > **perform,duties / promise**  
 > You should perform your duties / promise.   
 > 你应当履行职责/诺言。  

 > **perform an experiment / an operation / a miracle**  
 > perform an experiment / an operation / a miracle  
 > 做实验/做手术/创造奇迹  

### 2.*高义频：* **vt & vi表演；演出：**  

 > The band was going to perform at our local theatre.  
 > 乐队将在我们当地剧院演出。  
 > 来源：2011 山东改  

 > I’ve never seen a Shakespeare’s play performed so wonderfully.  
 > 我从没看过表演得如此好的莎士比亚戏剧。  

 > perform perfectly on the piano   
 > 熟练地演奏钢琴  

### 3.*高义频：* **vi 表现；运转：**  

 > **performed well**  
 > He was disappointed because he had not performed well in the sports meeting.  
 > 他很失望，因为他在运动会上表现不佳。  

 > **performing,poorly**  
 > The machine is performing very poorly.   
 > 机器运转非常不正常。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
Listening to music at home is one thing, going to hear it ________ (perform) live is quite another.  
##### 来源：2015 浙江改  
##### 答案 (being) performed

 > **give a live performance**

 > put on a performance of Hamlet   
 > 上演《哈姆雷特》

 > **good performance**  
 > My good performance in the job interview left me optimistic about my future.

 > 来源：2014 安徽  

 > **poor performance of**  
 > He criticized the recent poor performance of the company.   
 > 他批评公司近期业绩不佳。

# ***\*permanent*** adj
英音 'pɜːmənənt     美音 'pɜːrmənənt  

| 词频 1 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **永久的；长久的**  
反义词 temporary / impermanent： 

 > There are no permanent displays in this museum and exhibitions change all the time.   
 > 馆内没有永久性的展览，展品都是不断更换的。  
 > 来源：人教⑥ – 1  

 > a permanent job   
 > 固定工作  


派生词汇
---
permanently /'pɜːmənəntli/ adv   

真题解析
---
##### 题目  
An unhappy childhood may have some negative effects on a person’s character, however, they are not always ________.   
A.practical   
B.avoidable  
C.permanent   
D.beneficial  
##### 来源：2011 湖北  
##### 答案 C  
  

# ***\*permission*** n
英音 pə'mɪʃn     美音 pər'mɪʃn  

| 词频 3 | 口语 2 | 书面 1 |  

用法点拨  [U]

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **许可；准许：**  

 > **ask permission**  
 > ask permission  
 > 请求许可  

 > **without permission**  
 > He entered the room without permission.   
 > 他未经许可就进了房间。  

- permission to do sth:

 > Give yourself permission to rest when you’re tired.  
 > 当你疲倦的时候要让自己休息。  
 > 来源：2010 安徽  


# ***\*permit*** v  重难点词汇
英音 pə'mɪt     美音 pər'mɪt  

| 词频 4 | 书面 1 |  

用法点拨  [正式用语]

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **许可；准许**  
英译 to allow sth to happen or sb to do sth
反义词 forbid： 

 > **permitted,in**  
 > Mobile phone conversations are not permitted anywhere in the library.  
 > 图书馆内任何地方都禁止使用手机打电话。  
 > 来源：2013 天津  

- permit sb sth:

 > Please permit me a few words.   
 > 请允许我说几句。  

- permit sb to do sth:

 > He permitted me to retake the test, and I pulled my grade to an A.   
 > 他允许我重新参加考试，我的成绩因此提高到了A。  

### 2.*高义频：* **(使) 成为可能：**  

 > **if time permits**  
 > I’ll pick you up at the airport if time permits.   
 > 如果时间允许的话，我会去机场接你。  

 > **weather permitting**  
 > We’ll start tomorrow, weather permitting (= if the weather is good enough).  
 > 天气允许的话，我们明天出发。  

 > **permit you to**  
 > Cash machines permit you to withdraw money at any time.  
 > 取款机可以让你随时取款。  

Notes: permit和allow的用法相似，permit是正式用语；指天气、时间等客观因素允许时，只能用permit。  

真题解析
---
##### 题目  
I was the first Western TV reporter ________ (permit) to film a special unit caring for pandas rescued from starvation in the wild.  
##### 来源：2016 全国  
##### 答案 permitted  
  
##### 题目  
The party will be held in the garden, weather ________ (permit).   
##### 来源：2012 全国改  
##### 答案 permitting  
  
##### 题目  
Passengers are permitted ________ (carry) only one piece of hand luggage onto the plane.  
##### 来源：2011 天津改  
##### 答案 to carry

# ***\*personal*** adj
英音 'pɜːsənl     美音 'pɜːrsənl  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **[只用于名词前] 个人的；私人的：**  

 > **personal view / opinion**  
 > a personal view / opinion  
 > 个人的观点  

 > personal taste / qualities  
 > 个人喜好 / 人品  

 > **personal experience**  
 > The novel is written from personal experience.   
 > 这部小说是根据个人的亲身经历而写的。  

 > His personal life is a mystery to his colleagues.   
 > 对同事们来说，他的私生活是个谜。

 > make a personal visit   
 > 亲自拜访

# ***\*persuade*** vt  重难点词汇
英音 pə'sweɪd     美音 pər'sweɪd  

| 词频 4 | 口语 1 | 书面 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **说服；劝服 (talk into)：**  

 > She is always easily persuaded.   
 > 她总是很容易被说服。  

- persuade sb to do sth:

 > She persuaded me to go to a dental school.  
 > 她说服了我去牙科学校学习。  

- persuade sb into (doing) sth:

 > I managed to persuade my classmates into accepting my idea.  
 > 我设法说服了我的同学接受我的想法。  
 > 来源：2015 浙江书面表达  

- persuade sb out of (doing) sth:

 > We persuaded him out of his foolish plan.   
 > 我们说服了他放弃那项愚蠢的计划。  

Notes: 在表示“劝说”，但不一定“劝服”时，用try to persuade。  
 > She would try to persuade local business leaders to contribute money to the cause.  
 > 她会劝说当地的商界领导人为该事业捐款。  
 > 来源：2017 北京改  

### 2.*高义频：* **使相信；使信服 (convince)：**  

- persuade sb of sth:

 > I’m persuaded of his honesty.   
 > 我相信他是诚实的。  

- persuade sb + that 从句:

 > I persuaded him that I was telling the truth.   
 > 我使他相信我讲的是实情。  


派生词汇
---
persuasion /pə'sweɪʒn/ n [U]   
persuasive /pə'sweɪsɪv/ adj   

真题解析
---
##### 题目  
If she doesn’t want to go, nothing you can say will ________ (说服) her.  
##### 来源：2012 全国改  
##### 答案 persuade

# ***\*phone*** v
英音 fəʊn     美音 foʊn  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **(给某人) 打电话：**  

 > We’ll phone you if we have any news.   
 > 如有任何消息，我们会给你打电话。  

 > He phoned to invite me out for dinner.   
 > 他打电话请我出去吃饭。  


# ***\*phone*** n
英音 fəʊn     美音 foʊn  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 2 |  

用法点拨  [C]

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **电话机；电话：**  

 > a cell phone  
 > 手机  

 > **answer,pick up the phone**  
 > answer / hang up / pick up the phone   
 > 接/挂断/拿起电话  


固定搭配
---
## \*(be) on the phone
1.**在打电话：**  

 > I couldn’t get through to Hannah. Her brother was talking on the phone all the time!  
 > 我打不通汉纳的电话，她哥哥一直在打电话。  
 > 来源：2008 湖南改

# ***\*physical*** adj
英音 'fɪzɪkl     美音 'fɪzɪkl  

| 词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **物理的；自然的：**  

 > a physical change  
 > 物理变化  

### 2.*高义频：* **物质的；实物的：**  

 > **physical world / environment**  
 > the physical world / environment   
 > 物质世界/客观环境  

 > Physical things are those you can see and touch.   
 > 物质的东西是看得见、摸得着的。  

### 3.*高义频：* **身体的；肉体的**  
反义词 mental： 

 > a physical disability   
 > 生理缺陷  

 > To keep fit, we often take part in physical exercise.  
 > 为了保持健康，我们经常参加体育锻炼。  


派生词汇
---
physically /'fɪzɪkli/ adv

# ***\*pick*** vt  重难点词汇
英音 pɪk     美音 pɪk  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **摘；采：**  

 > pick grapes / flowers  
 > 采摘葡萄/采花  

### 2.*高义频：* **摘掉；剔除：**  

 > pick one’s teeth   
 > 剔牙  

 > He picked the nuts off the top of the cake.   
 > 他把蛋糕上面的果仁拿掉。  

### 3.*高义频：* **挑选；选择：**  

 > **picked,words**  
 > He picked his words carefully.   
 > 他用词细心谨慎。  

- pick sb to do sth:

 > When I was in the third grade, I was picked to be the princess in the school play.  
 > 在三年级时，我被选为校园剧中的公主。  

- pick sb / sth for sth:

 > Ben was picked for the soccer team.  
 > 本被选进了足球队。  

#### 辨析 select, choose, pick
三者都有“选择”之意。  


固定搭配
---
## \*pick sb’s pocket
1.**扒窃；掏包**  

## \*pick on 
1.**挑选；故意挑剔：**  

 > Why do you pick on me to do the unpleasant jobs?  
 > 你为什么找我做这些令人不愉快的工作?  

 > Why pick on my family?   
 > 为什么拿我的家庭说事？  
 > 来源：2011 江西  

## \*pick out
1.*高义频：* **选出；拣出：**  

 > Perhaps you can help me pick out a pair of jeans, since you are an expert.  
 > 因为你是个行家，也许你能帮我挑选一条牛仔裤。  
 > 来源：2014 四川  

 > His story was picked out as the best by the judges.  
 > 他的小说被评委们评为最佳作品。  

2.*低义频：* **区别出；辨别出：**  

 > See if you can pick me out in this photo.   
 > 看你能不能从这张照片上认出我来。  

 > There have been experiments where people could pick out a particular smell.   
 > 有实验证明，人们可以辨认出某种特定的气味。  
 > 来源：2008 北京  

## \*pick up
1.*高义频：* **提起；拿起：**  

- 拿起；拾起：

 > The phone rang and I picked it up.   
 > 电话响了，我接了起来。  

 > I picked up the rubbish and threw it into the trash can.   
 > 我把垃圾拾起来，扔进垃圾桶。  

 > She went over to the crying child and picked her up.  
 > 她走到啼哭的孩子身边，把她抱了起来。  

- (车辆等) 中途搭 (人) (collect)；中途带 (货)：

 > I’ve got to pick up my daughter from school at four o’clock.   
 > 我四点钟得去学校接女儿。  
 > 来源：北师大③ – 9  

 > Buses pick up and drop off people at different places on the route.   
 > 公交车在其线路上不同的地方让人们上下车。  

- 营救；救起：

 > Twenty men fell into the water and were picked up by other boats.  
 > 二十人落水后，被其他船只救起。  
 > 来源：外研⑥ – 6  

2.*高义频：* **得到：**  

- (偶然地、无意地) 得到 / 买到；学会 (语言)：

 > pick up bad habits   
 > 染上了坏习惯  

 > He picked up a few dollars by doing part-time jobs.  
 > 他靠兼职挣了几个钱。  

 > She picked up Japanese when she was in Japan. Now she can speak it freely.   
 > 她在日本的时候学会了日语，现在她日语讲得很流利。  

 > We managed to pick up a few bargains in the market.  
 > 我们从市场上买到了几件便宜货。  

- 接收到：

 > We were able to pick up the BBC World Service.   
 > 我们能收听到英国广播公司的国际广播节目。  

3.*高义频：* **取回；收集：**  

 > I’ll pick up the tickets at lunchtime tomorrow.   
 > 我明天午饭时间去取票。  
 > 来源：北师大② – 5  

 > pick up the heat    
 > 收集热量  
 > 来源：2009 安徽  

4.*低义频：* **重提 (话题)；恢复 (状态等)：**  

 > He picks up this theme again in later chapters of the book.   
 > 在该书的后几章，他又重回到这个主题上。  

 > **things are picking up**  
 > We’ve been through a hard time, but things are picking up again now.  
 > 我们经历了一段困难的日子，不过现在情况又好转了。  

5.*低义频：* **提高；(风) 变大：**  

 > **picked up speed**  
 > The train picked up speed.   
 > 火车提速了。  

 > The wind had picked up, and dark clouds rolled across the sky.   
 > 风愈刮愈大，天空中乌云密布。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
It’s surprising that your brother picked ________ Russian so quickly — he hasn’t lived there very long.   
##### 来源：2012 四川改  
##### 答案 up  
  
##### 题目  
Sam picked ________ some knowledge of the computer just by watching others working on it.   
##### 来源：2010 山东改  
##### 答案 up  
  
##### 题目  
It was so dark in the cinema that I could hardly pick ________ my friend.   
##### 来源：2007 四川改  
##### 答案 out

 > 来源：2014 广东

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **堆；摞：**  

 > a pile of books

### 2.*高义频：* **大量：**  

 > **piles of**  
 > Most of the students’time was spent at school doing piles of homework.   
 > 学生的大部分时间都用来在学校做大量的作业。  
 > 来源：2008 湖北改  

 > **piles of**  
 > We received piles of letters from readers.   
 > 我们收到了大量的读者来信。

英音 paɪl     美音 paɪl  

| 词频 4 |  

英文释义
---

 > Please help us pile these books.

 > **piled,with**  
 > He piled his plate with as much food as he could.  
 > 他在盘子上盛了尽可能多的食物。

---

# ***\*pity*** n
英音 'pɪti     美音 'pɪti  

| 词频 4 | 口语 1 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **[U] 同情；怜悯：**  

 > We helped her out of pity.  
 > 我们出于怜悯帮助了她。  

 > **took pity on**  
 > The owner of the house took pity on us and let us come in out of the rain.  
 > 房主同情我们，让我们进屋避雨。  

### 2.*高义频：* **[C] [用单数] 可惜的事；憾事 (shame)：**  

 > **What a pity**  
 > What a pity!   
 > 真可惜！  

 > **It was a pity,that**  
 > It was a pity (that) you could not come.   
 > 你不能来真是遗憾。  

 > The pity was that the winner couldn’t be there to receive the prize.   
 > 遗憾的是获奖者不能前来领奖。  
 > 来源：2009 福建改  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
— Can you come to a party on Saturday, Peter?
— Oh, what pity! I’m already going out, I’m afraid.  
##### 来源：2015 安徽改 改错  
##### 答案 pity 前加 a  
  
##### 题目  
— The Modern Art Exhibition in the City Museum has been cancelled.
— Oh, no! It’s pity.  
##### 来源：2012 重庆改 改错  
##### 答案 pity 前加 a

# ***\*place*** n
英音 pleɪs     美音 pleɪs  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

用法点拨  [C]

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **地方；地点；部位：**  

 > Birds seek safe places before a storm.   
 > 鸟儿会在暴风雨来临前寻找安全的地方。  

 > a sore place on the leg   
 > 腿上的疼痛处  

### 2.*高义频：* **住所；场所：**  

 > **my place**  
 > Some of my friends are coming for dinner at my place.  
 > 有几个朋友要来我家吃饭。  
 > 来源：2015 浙江  

### 3.*低义频：* **位置；地位；身份：**  

 > Working has a very important place in all our lives.  
 > 工作在我们生活中占据着重要位置。  

### 4.*低义频：* **资格；名额；机会：**  

 > get a place in a law firm   
 > 在律师事务所工作  

 > They might just have a place left on the writing course.  
 > 写作课或许正好还有一个剩余名额。  
 > 来源：2013 全国  

### 5.*高义频：* **名次：**  

 > Luck was smiling on me that day as I won first place in the competition.   
 > 那天幸运女神向我微笑，我获得了比赛第一名。  
 > 来源：译林⑥ – 1  


固定搭配
---
## \*in place 
1.**在适当的位置；适当的；准备妥当：**  

 > The ropes hold you in place so that you don’t fall.   
 > 绳子会把你固定在适当的位置，这样你就不会掉下去。  
 > 来源：2008 安徽  

 > After the dinner, an expression of thanks to the host would be in place.   
 > 饭后向主人道声谢是比较合适的。  

 > The service could be in place by the end of the year.  
 > 这项服务将于年底准备就绪。  

## \*in place of 
1.**代替；取代 (in sb’s / sth’s place)：**  

 > You can use yoghurt in place of cream to make this salad.   
 > 你可以用酸奶替代奶油来做这道沙拉。  

 > If I refused to go, they would send someone else in my place.   
 > 如果我不去，他们会派其他人代替我的。  

## \*out of place 
1.**不在合适的位置上；不合适的；不相称的：**  

 > Some of these files seem to be out of place.   
 > 有些文件似乎没放对地方。  

 > I felt completely out of place among all these successful people.   
 > 夹在这些成功人士中间，我觉得自己格格不入。  

## \*take place 
1.**发生；举行：**  

 > Great changes have taken place in the way people communicate in recent years.  
 > 近年来，人们交流的方式发生了巨大的变化。  

#### 辨析 happen, take place
二者都可指“发生”。  

## \*take the place of 
1.**代替 (take sb’s / sth’s place):**  

 > Computers have taken the place of typewriters in offices.  
 > 在办公室里，电脑已取代了打字机。  

 > She couldn’t attend the meeting so her assistant took her place.  
 > 她不能出席会议，所以她的助手代替了她。  


# ***\*place*** vt
英音 pleɪs     美音 pleɪs  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **放置；安置：**  

 > He placed his fingers on the piano keys.   
 > 他把手指放在钢琴键上。  

### 2.*高义频：* **发出 (订单)；登 (广告)：**  

 > **place,order,advertisement**  
 > place an order / advertisement   
 > 下订单/登广告  

### 3.*低义频：* **定名次：**  

 > He was placed third in last Saturday’s race.   
 > 在上周六的比赛中，他名列第三。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
The furniture, with its modern style and bright colors, suits modern houses and their gardens, but looks ________ (不相称的) in the garden of a traditional home.  
##### 来源：2012 湖北改  
##### 答案 out of place

# ***\*plain*** adj
英音 pleɪn     美音 pleɪn  

| 词频 3 | 口语 2 | 书面 1 | 阅读 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **清楚的；明白的；易懂的 (clear / obvious)：**  

 > a plain fact   
 > 明显的事实  

 > **in plain English**  
 > The story is written in plain English.   
 > 故事用简单易懂的英语写成。  

### 2.*高义频：* **简朴的；简单的；单色的**  
英译 without anything added or without decoration：

 > a plain but elegant dress   
 > 朴素淡雅的连衣裙  

 > plain yoghurt   
 > 原味酸奶  

 > The bike is in plain black and easy to ride.  
 > 这辆自行车是纯黑色的，非常好骑。  
 > 来源：2012 重庆书面表达  

### 3.*低义频：* **平常的；相貌平平的：**  

 > a policeman in plain clothes   
 > 便衣警察  

 > Her face is plain, but she has a nice smile!   
 > 她长相普通，但笑容很甜美！  

### 4.*高义频：* **坦白的；直率的：**  

 > Let us be plain with you.  
 > 我们坦白对你说吧。

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **计划；筹划：**  

 > planned economy and market economy   
 > 计划经济与市场经济  

 > **as planned**  
 > To complete the project as planned, we’ll have to work two more hours a day.  
 > 为了按计划完成这个项目，我们将不得不每天加班两个小时。  
 > 来源：2008 湖南  

 > Planning is good, but doing is better.  
 > 要计划，更要有行动。  
 > 来源：2016 浙江书面表达  

### 2.*高义频：* **打算：**  

- plan on (doing) sth:

 > She is planning on introducing me to her parents.  
 > 她正打算把我介绍给她的父母。  
 > 来源：2008 广东  

- plan to do sth:

 > Judy and I plan to play table tennis tomorrow.   
 > 我和朱迪打算明天打乒乓球。  
 > 来源：2008 天津  

### 3.*高义频：* **设计 (design)：**  

 > plan an essay / a garden   
 > 构思文章/设计花园

# ***\*play*** v
英音 pleɪ     美音 pleɪ  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

用法点拨  vt & vi

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **做 (游戏)；玩耍；娱乐：**  

 > Show us how to play the game, will you?   
 > 你能教我们怎么玩这个游戏吗？  

 > The streets I used to play in are jammed with cars now.  
 > 我过去经常玩耍的街道如今堵满了汽车。  
 > 来源：2010 浙江  

 > **playing with**  
 > Kathy picked up a lot of Spanish by playing with the native boys and girls.  
 > 通过跟当地孩子一起玩，凯西学会了很多西班牙语。  

### 2.*高义频：* **参加 (体育活动、比赛等)：**  

 > play basketball / volleyball  
 > 打篮球/排球  

 > play cards / bridge  
 > 打纸牌 / 桥牌  

 > **play against**  
 > The Houston Rockets will play against the Los Angeles Lakers.   
 > 休斯敦火箭队将对阵洛杉矶湖人队。  

### 3.*高义频：* **弹奏；演奏；扮演；演出：**  

 > play the guitar   
 > 弹吉他  

 > They’re playing the National Anthem.   
 > 他们在奏国歌。  

 > **played a,part in**  
 > Last year he played a major part in the school play.  
 > 去年，他在校园剧中扮演了一个重要角色。  
 > 来源：人教⑦ – 1  

 > This scene doesn’t play so well.   
 > 这一场演得并不好。  

### 4.*高义频：* **播放 (唱片、磁带等)：**  

 > Play their new CD for me, please.   
 > 请把他们的新唱片放给我听一下吧。  


固定搭配
---
## \*play with
1.**玩弄：**  

 > Stop playing with your food!  
 > 别老是摆弄食物！  


# ***\*play*** n
英音 pleɪ     美音 pleɪ  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **[U] 玩耍；游戏；嬉戏：**  

 > **at play**  
 > at play   
 > 在玩耍  

 > Play is very important to a child’s development.   
 > 游戏对孩子的成长十分重要。  

### 2.*高义频：* **[C] 戏剧；剧本：**  

 > go to a play   
 > 去看戏  

 > **put on / perform a play**  
 > put on / perform a play   
 > 演戏

# ***\*pleasant*** adj
英音 'pleznt     美音 'pleznt  

| 词频 4 | 口语 1 | 书面 1 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **令人愉快的；舒适的 (nice)；礼貌而友善的：**  

 > I hope you’ll have a pleasant journey.  
 > 祝你 (们) 旅途愉快！  
 > 来源：人教① – 3  

 > **It was pleasant to**  
 > It was pleasant to sit in a sidewalk cafe and watch people pass.   
 > 坐在路边咖啡馆看着人来人往真是惬意。  

 > He had a pleasant manner and was a gifted public speaker.  
 > 他态度和蔼，是一个有天赋的演说家。  
 > 来源：2010 广东  


派生词汇
---
pleasantly /'plezntli/ adv   

# ***\*please*** v
英音 pliːz     美音 pliːz  

| 词频 5 | 书面 1 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **(使) 高兴；(使) 满意；讨好：**  

 > It pleases me that he should want to talk about his worries.  
 > 他愿和我谈谈他的烦心事，我很高兴。  

 > **is hard to please**  
 > She is hard to please. Everything has to be perfect.  
 > 让她满意很难，一切都得完美才行。  

### 2.*低义频：* **喜欢；愿意：**  

 > **as you please**  
 > You may stay as long as you please.   
 > 你想待多久就待多久。  


派生词汇
---
pleasing /'pliːzɪŋ/ adj   
 > **pleasing to the eye**  
 > a design that is pleasing to the eye  
 > 悦目的设计  


# ***\*please*** int
英音 pliːz     美音 pliːz  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **[表示有礼貌地请求对方] 请；好吗：**  

 > Would / Could / Will you please …?   
 > 你…好吗？  

### 2.*高义频：* **[表示礼貌地接受] 好；谢谢：**  

 > — Would you like some more?  
 > 还要来点吗？  

 > — Yes, please.  
 > 好的，谢谢。  
 > 来源：2013 四川  


# ***\*pleased*** adj
英音 pliːzd     美音 pliːzd  

| 词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 1 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **[不用于名词前]高兴的；满意的：**  

- (be) pleased to do sth:

 > Her parents were so pleased to get the news that she won the prize.   
 > 得知她获奖的消息，她的父母非常高兴。  
 > 来源：人教③ – 5  

- (be) pleased + (that) 从句：

 > Everyone is pleased that you’ve decided to come to the party.   
 > 你决定来参加聚会大家都十分高兴。  

- (be) pleased with:

 > I am very pleased with the quality of your work.   
 > 我对你的工作质量很满意。  


固定搭配
---
## \*(be) pleased with oneself 
1.**自鸣得意**  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
— I’m very ________ (please) with my own cooking. It looks nice and smells delicious.
— Mm, it does have a pleasant smell.   
##### 来源：2002 京蒙皖改  
##### 答案 pleased  
  

# ***\*pleasure*** n
英音 'pleʒə(r)     美音 'pleʒər  

| 词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **[U] 快乐 (enjoyment)；娱乐：**  

 > **took pleasure in**  
 > From her teenage years, she took pleasure in writing short stories.   
 > 从十几岁起，她就喜欢写些小故事。  

### 2.*高义频：* **[C] 乐事；乐趣：**  

 > Giving is always a pleasure.  
 > 给予永远都是件乐事。  
 > 来源：2008 北京  

 > **a,pleasure to**  
 > It is a great pleasure to meet you students from England.  
 > 非常高兴认识你们这些从英国来的学生。  
 > 来源：人教⑧–5  

 > He enjoyed all the pleasures there were in life.   
 > 他享受生活中所有的乐趣。  


固定搭配
---
## \*for pleasure 
1.**作为消遣：**  

 > We read mainly for information, not for pleasure.   
 > 我们读书主要是为了获取信息，并非为了消遣。  

## \*it’s a pleasure / (it’s) my pleasure
1.**[用于对别人感谢的回答] 别客气；没什么：**  

 > — Thank you for coming to help us.   
 > 谢谢你来帮助我们。  

 > — It’s a pleasure. / My pleasure.  
 > 别客气。  

## \*with pleasure 
1.**高兴地；[用于应答] 非常乐意：**  

 > Invited into a friend’s home, you should accept with pleasure.  
 > 如果被邀请去朋友家做客，你应该高兴地接受。  

 > — Would you like to come and have lunch on Sunday?   
 > 你愿意周日来吃午餐吗？  

 > — With pleasure. I’d love to come.   
 > 当然了，我很乐意来。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
— Could you be so kind as to close the window?
— ________ (当然可以). (pleasure)  
##### 来源：2009 安徽改  
##### 答案 With pleasure  
  

# ***\*plenty*** pron
英音 'plenti     美音 'plenti  

| 词频 4 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **丰富；大量；充足：**  

 > — Would you like some more?   
 > 你再来点儿吗？  

 > — No, thanks. I’ve had plenty.   
 > 谢谢，不要了。我已经吃了很多。  


固定搭配
---
## \*plenty of 
1.**相当多的；充足的：**  

 > There are plenty of books on the shelf.   
 > 书架上有许多书。  

 > We always keep plenty of spare paper, in case we run out.  
 > 我们总是备有足够的纸张，以防用完。  

Notes: plenty of 可接可数或不可数名词，只用于肯定句。  

派生词汇
---
plentiful /'plentɪfl/ adj   

真题解析
---
##### 题目  
We always keep plenty ________ spare paper, in case we run out.  
##### 来源：2006 浙江改  
##### 答案 of

# ***\*point*** v  重难点词汇
英音 pɔɪnt     美音 pɔɪnt  

| 词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **[不用于被动语态] 用 (手指等) 指；指向：**  

- point at / to / towards sb / sth:

 > It is rude to point your finger at others.  
 > 用手指指他人是不礼貌的。  

### 2.*高义频：* **对准：**  

 > **pointed at**  
 > A hundred cameras were being pointed at her.   
 > 上百个相机对准了她。  

### 3.*高义频：* **面向；朝向：**  

 > **points in a,direction**  
 > The sign post points in a wrong direction.   
 > 路标指向错误的方向。  

 > **points to / towards**  
 > The needle of a compass always points to / towards the north.  
 > 罗盘的指针总指向北。  

### 4.*低义频：* **(意思上) 指向；暗示；表明：**  

 > **pointed to / towards**  
 > All the evidence pointed to / towards Tony as the thief.  
 > 所有证据都表明托尼是小偷。  


固定搭配
---
## \*point out
1.**把…指出来 (给看)；指出；指明：**  

 > **pointed out to**  
 > I pointed out to him where I used to live.  
 > 我把我过去住的地方指给他看。  

 > **pointed out that**  
 > He pointed out that the road was not safe in winter.  
 > 他指出这条路冬天不安全。  


# ***\*point*** n  重难点词汇
英音 pɔɪnt     美音 pɔɪnt  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **[C] 尖端；点；小数点：**  

 > the point of a pencil / knife   
 > 铅笔尖/刀尖  

 > The two lines cross at point C.   
 > 这两条线在C点相交。  

 > two point six   
 > 二点六(2.6)  

### 2.*高义频：* **[C] 时间点；地点：**  

 > **a turning / starting point**  
 > a turning / starting point  
 > 转折点/起点  

 > **a low / high point**  
 > a low / high point  
 > 低谷/巅峰  

 > **at some point**  
 > You’ll regret at some point in the future if you don’t study hard today.  
 > 如果你现在不好好学习，将来某个时候你就会后悔。  

 > **reached a point**  
 > I have reached a point in my life when / where I am supposed to make decisions of my own.  
 > 我到了人生中应该自己拿主意的时候。  
 > 来源：2009 浙江  

### 3.*高义频：* **[C] 观点；要点；特点：**  

 > **from,point of view**  
 > Whenever you buy a present, you should think about it from the receiver’s point of view.  
 > 每当你买礼物时，都应当从接受者的角度来考虑。  
 > 来源：2014 湖南  

 > **main points**  
 > Read the passage and get the main points of it.   
 > 阅读这篇文章并理解其要点。  

 > **that’s not the point**  
 > You didn’t intend to be late. But that’s not the point (= not the important thing).  
 > 你不想迟到，但那不是重点。  
 > 来源：2014 辽宁  

 > **make,point**  
 > He told a story, within which he tried to make his point.  
 > 故事中他提出了自己的观点。  
 > 来源：2015 湖北  

 > **strong / weak points**  
 > strong / weak points  
 > 强项/不足处  

### 4.*高义频：* **[C] (比赛或运动中的)分 (数)：**  

 > win a match by ten points to three   
 > 以10比3赢得比赛  

### 5.*高义频：* **[U] 意图；目的；理由**  
英译 the purpose or aim of sth：

 > **What’s the point**  
 > What’s the point of forcing him to do what he is unwilling to?   
 > 强迫他做不愿意做的事情有什么意义呢?  

 > **There’s no point in**  
 > There’s no point in getting angry.   
 > 生气是没有用的。  


固定搭配
---
## \*make a point of doing sth
1.**(即使费力也) 特意做某事：**  

 > He made a point of spending Saturdays with his children.   
 > 星期六他必定要和孩子们在一起。  

## \*on the point of 
1.**正要…的时候：**  

 > She was on the point of going out when the telephone rang.   
 > 她正要出去，电话铃响了。  

## \*to the point 
1.**中肯的；切题的：**  

 > Your advice is very much to the point.  
 > 你的建议很中肯。  

 > **get to the point**  
 > I wish you’d get to the point (= talk about the most important thing).  
 > 我希望你能切入正题。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
What’s the point, in your opinion, ________ helping him if he doesn’t make an effort to help himself?  
##### 来源：2011 江西改  
##### 答案 of  
  
##### 题目  
I like Mr Miner’s speech; it was clear and ________ the point.   
##### 来源：2008 辽宁改  
##### 答案 to

# ***\*poor*** adj
英音 pɔː(r); pʊə     美音 pɔːr  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **贫穷的；贫困的；贫乏的**  
反义词 rich 

 > as poor as a church mouse   
 > 一贫如洗  

 > the poor   
 > 穷人  

 > **poor in**  
 > That country is poor in natural resources.  
 > 那个国家自然资源匮乏。  

### 2.*高义频：* **不善于的；差的；体弱的：**  

 > **in poor health**  
 > He was in poor health.  
 > 他身体不好。  

 > **poor at**  
 > I am poor at sports.  
 > 我不擅长运动。  

### 3.*高义频：* **可怜的；不幸的：**  

 > The poor man lost both his legs in the accident.  
 > 这个不幸的人在事故中失去了双腿。  


派生词汇
---

##### 来源：2019 全国  
##### 答案 poorly

# ***\*popular*** adj  重难点词汇
英音 'pɒpjələ(r)     美音 'pɑːpjələr  

| 词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **流行的；受欢迎的**  
反义词 unpopular： 

 > **increasingly popular**  
 > Online voting becomes increasingly popular, and many competitions get people involved in it.  
 > 在线投票越来越盛行，很多比赛都让人们参与进来投票。  
 > 来源：2016 江苏书面表达  

## \*be popular with / among
1.**为…喜欢；受…欢迎：**  

 > The mobile phone is fashionable and convenient to carry, so it is very popular with youngsters.  
 > 这款手机样式新颖、携带方便，深受年轻人的欢迎。  

 > Smart and pretty, Kate is very popular among her friends.  
 > 凯特既聪明又漂亮，深受朋友们的喜爱。  

### 2.*高义频：* **公众的；大众化的；通俗的：**  

 > **a popular belief / opinion**  
 > a popular belief / opinion  
 > 普遍的观念/民意  

 > What we need most are popular science books.  
 > 我们最需要的是科普类图书。  
 > 来源：2014 浙江书面表达  

 > in popular language   
 > 用通俗的语言  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
This magazine is very popular ________ young people, who like its content and style.   
##### 来源：2007 湖北改  
##### 答案 with / among

# ***\*population*** n  重难点词汇
英音 ˌpɒpju'leɪʃn     美音 ˌpɑːpju'leɪʃn  

| 词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 |  

用法点拨  [C]

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **人口；人口数量：**  

 > a country with the ageing population   
 > 人口老龄化的国家  

 > The Bai ethnic group has a population of around two million, 90% of whom live in Yunnan.   
 > 白族人口大约有200万，其中的90%居住在云南。  
 > 来源： 外研⑦ – 5  

### 2.*高义频：* **(某事物的) 总数；(人的) 全体：**  

 > the dolphin population   
 > 海豚总数  

 > The whole population of the town came out to welcome him.   
 > 整个镇上的居民都出来欢迎他。  

Notes: 问“…有多少人口？”时，要使用what，不能用how many或how much；修饰人口多少的形容词不用many或few，而用large或small。  
 > What is the population of Zhejiang Province?   
 > 浙江省有多少人口？  

 > China has the largest population in the world.   
 > 世界上中国人口最多。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
The population of Jiangsu ________ to more than twice what it was in 1949. The figure is now approaching 74 million. 
  
A.has grown  
B.have grown  
C.grew  
D.are growing  
##### 来源：2009 江苏  
##### 答案 A

# ***\*position*** n  重难点词汇
英音 pə'zɪʃn     美音 pə'zɪʃn  

| 词频 4 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **位置；方位；(恰当或正确的) 位置：**  

 > Can you show me the position of the city on the map?  
 > 你能在地图上给我指出那个城市的位置吗？  

 > **in position**  
 > The orchestra were all in position, waiting for the conductor.   
 > 管弦乐队队员都已各就各位，等待着指挥。  

### 2.*高义频：* **姿势；(物体所指的) 方向：**  

 > **comfortable position**  
 > Lie in a comfortable position.   
 > 以一种舒适的姿势躺下。  

 > They had to stand for hours without changing position.   
 > 他们得一动不动地站几个小时。  

 > Keep the box in an upright position.   
 > 把盒子竖着放。  

### 3.*高义频：* **地位；身份：**  

 > **The,position of**  
 > The social position of each character influences the way they behave to each other.  
 > 每个人的社会地位影响他们对待彼此的方式。  
 > 来源：人教⑧ – 4  

 > a man of position   
 > 有身份的人  

### 4.*高义频：* **[正式用语] 职位；职务 a job (post)：**  

 > **applying for,position**  
 > He is thinking of applying for the position of Chief Editor.  
 > 他正在考虑申请主编的职位。  

 > **takes / holds,position**  
 > Bruce takes / holds the position of sales manager in a large company.   
 > 布鲁斯在一家大公司担任销售经理的职务。  

### 5.*低义频：* **(比赛中的) 名次：**  

 > **finished,in third position**  
 > She finished the race in third position.   
 > 她在比赛中得了第三名。  

### 6.*高义频：* **处境；状况**  
英译 the state or situation that sb / sth is in：

 > **in,position**  
 > What would you do if in my position?   
 > 如果处于我这种状况你会怎么办？  

 > **not in a position**  
 > I’m afraid I am not in a position to help you.   
 > 我恐怕帮不了你。  

### 7.*高义频：* **立场；观点；态度**  
英译 an opinion on or an attitude towards a particular subject (attitude)：

 > **take,position on**  
 > When the time comes to make a decision and take a position on an issue, allow for the contributions of each member of the group.   
 > 就某个问题作出决定和发表意见的时候，要允许组内每个成员提出自己的想法。  
 > 来源：2008 江苏  

 > **reconsider,position**  
 > I hope you’ll reconsider your position.   
 > 我希望你能重新考虑你的立场。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
From their ________ (位置) on the top of the TV Tower, visitors can have a better view of the city.  
##### 来源：2009 陕西改  
##### 答案 position  
  

# ***\*position*** v  重难点词汇
英音 pə'zɪʃn     美音 pə'zɪʃn  

| 词频 4 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **放置；安放：**  

 > **positioned myself**  
 > I positioned myself to take the best photo of the sea view.  
 > 我站好位置以便拍到最美的海景照片。  
 > 来源：2017 天津改  


# ***\*positive*** adj
英音 'pɒzətɪv     美音 'pɑːzətɪv  

| 词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **正面的；积极乐观的；有益的**  
反义词 negative： 

 > **positive effects**  
 > I believe that the Internet has positive effects on our lives.   
 > 我认为互联网对我们的生活有正面的影响。  
 > 来源：译林⑦ – 3  

 > **positive attitudes**  
 > People with high EQs usually have positive attitudes towards life.   
 > 高情商的人往往有着积极的生活态度。  

### 2.*高义频：* **确实的；确信的：**  

 > a positive fact   
 > 确信无疑的事实  

 > **positive about**  
 > She was quite positive about the amount of money involved.   
 > 她对所涉及的钱数十分肯定。  

 > I am positive that I gave you his address.   
 > 我肯定把他的地址给你了。  

### 3.*低义频：* **正的；阳性的**  
反义词 negative： 

 > a positive number   
 > 正数  

 > **tested positive**  
 > Anyone, once tested positive for the bird flu virus, will receive free medical treatment from our government.  
 > 任何人一旦被检测出禽流感病毒呈阳性，将获得政府提供的免费医疗。  
 > 来源：2013 福建改  


# ***\*possess*** vt
英音 pə'zes     美音 pə'zes  

| 词频 3 | 书面 1 | 阅读 2 |  

用法点拨  [正式用语] [不用于进行时]

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **拥有；占有；具有**  
英译 to have or own sth：

 > Happiness is not wishing for what we don’t have, but enjoying what we do possess.  
 > 幸福不是期求所缺，而是享受所有。  
 > 来源：2013 天津改  

 > He learned that horses possess many qualities that make them an excellent choice for guiding the blind.  
 > 他了解到马具有许多特质，这使得它们成为导盲的极佳选择。  


# ***\*possession*** n
英音 pə'zeʃn     美音 pə'zeʃn  

| 词频 3 | 书面 1 | 阅读 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **拥有；占有：**  

 > **came into possession**  
 > When her father died, she came into possession of a large fortune.   
 > 父亲去世后，她继承了一大笔财产。  

 > The possession of a happiest man may not be the best, but he knows how to fully enjoy what he has.  
 > 最幸福的人所拥有的不一定是最好的，但他懂得充分享受自己所拥有的。  

### 2.*高义频：* **所有物；财产 (belongings)：**  

 > Having been cheated by that company, he lost all his possessions.   
 > 被那家公司所骗，他失去了所有的财产。  
 > 来源：人教⑧ – 4  


固定搭配
---
## \*in possession of 
1.**占有；拥有：**  

 > Foreign visitors are required to be in possession of a passport.    
 > 外国游客必须持有护照。  

## \*in the possession of 
1.**为…所有：**  

 > That picture is in the possession of Tom.  
 > 那张画为汤姆所有。  

## \*take possession of 
1.**占有；拥有；占领：**  

 > We’ve already bought the house but we won’t take possession of it until May.   
 > 我们已经买了房子，但要到五月份才能拿到。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
Technical progress would put our firm in ________ (possess) of the home market.   
##### 来源：2007 陕西  
##### 答案 possession  
  

# ***\*possibility*** n
英音 ˌpɒsə'bɪləti     美音 ˌpɑːsə'bɪləti  

| 词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **可能性；可能：**  

 > **possibility of**  
 > Is there any possibility of our getting there in time?  
 > 我们有可能及时赶到那里吗？  

 > **a possibility that**  
 > There is a possibility that we will travel to China this Easter holiday.   
 > 这次复活节假期我们有可能去中国旅游。  
 > 来源：北师大⑤ – 13  

 > **possibility that**  
 > There’s no possibility that any of us will ever forget.  
 > 我们绝不可能忘记。  

### 2.*高义频：* **可能的办法：**  

 > **possibilities,of**  
 > possibilities for / of reducing costs   
 > 降低成本的可能方法  

### 3.*低义频：* **发展前途；潜在价值：**  

 > I saw great possibilities in the scheme from the beginning.  
 > 我从一开始就看到这计划很有前途。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
There is no possibility ________ Bob can win the first prize in the match.
  
##### 来源：2001 上海春改  
##### 答案 that  
  

# ***\*possible*** adj
英音 'pɒsəbl     美音 'pɑːsəbl  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **可能的**  
反义词 impossible: 

 > Anything is possible.  
 > 一切皆有可能。  

- it is possible (for sb) to do sth:

 > It is possible for him to accomplish the task.   
 > 他有可能完成这项任务。  

- it is possible + (that) 从句：

 > It is possible that we have met before.   
 > 我们可能以前见过。  
 > 来源：外研④ – 7  

### 2.*高义频：* **合理的；可接受的**  
英译 reasonable or acceptable in a particular situation：

 > There are several possible explanations.   
 > 有几种合理的解释。  

### 3.*低义频：* **[用于形容词后表示强调] 最...的：**  

 > **best possible**  
 > It was the best possible surprise anyone could have given me.   
 > 那是我曾感受过的最大的惊喜。  

 > **last possible**  
 > Don’t leave your packing until the last possible moment.   
 > 别把打点行李拖到最后一刻。  


固定搭配
---
## \*as ... as possible 
1.**尽可能...地：**  

 > Try to make your poster as attractive as possible.  
 > 使你的海报尽可能地吸引人。  

 > We must take action as quickly as possible now.  
 > 我们现在必须尽快采取行动。  
 > 来源：2015 湖北改  

 > You have to search for as many opportunities as possible to practice listening.   
 > 你要寻找尽可能多的机会练习听力。  
 > 来源：人教⑦ – 5  

## \*if possible 
1.**如果可能的话：**  

 > I want to avoid the rush hour traffic if possible.  
 > 如有可能，我想避开交通高峰期。  

## \*whenever / wherever possible
1.**只要有可能；一有机会：**  

 > Use public transport whenever possible (= when you can).  
 > 只要有可能，就用公共交通工具。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
Get an early start and try to be as productive ________ possible before lunch.  
##### 来源：2016 全国  
##### 答案 as  
  
##### 题目  
Raymond’s parents wanted him to have the ________ (good) possible education.  
##### 来源：2014 全国改  
##### 答案 best  
  
##### 题目  
— Have you got any particular plans for the coming holiday?
— Yes. ________ (如果可能的话), I’m going to visit some homes for the old in the city.  
##### 来源：2008 安徽改  
##### 答案 If possible  
  

# ***\*possibly*** adv
英音 'pɒsəbli     美音 'pɑːsəbli  

| 词频 4 | 口语 3 | 书面 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **可能；也许(maybe / perhaps)：**  

 > He could possibly be the most beautiful baby I’d ever seen.   
 > 他可能是我见过的最漂亮的婴儿。  
 > 来源：2008 全国  

### 2.*高义频：* **无论如何；竟然：**  

 > **can’t possibly**  
 > I can’t possibly accept your advice.   
 > 无论如何我都不能接受你的建议。  

 > How can you possibly miss the news? It has been on TV all day long.   
 > 你怎么会没看到这条新闻？电视上一整天都在播呢。  

### 3.*高义频：* **尽可能：**  

 > I’ll call you back as soon as I possibly can.   
 > 我会尽早给你回电话。  


固定搭配
---
## \*could you possibly
1.**... [表示郑重的请求] 您能…吗：**  

 > Could you possibly ask her to bring along that book?  
 > 您能让她把那本书带来吗？  
 > 来源：2008 天津

# ***\*power*** n  重难点词汇
英音 'paʊə(r)     美音 'paʊər  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **能力；[可用复数] (生理) 机能：**  

 > **do everything in my power**  
 > I will do everything in my power to help you.  
 > 我会尽全力帮助你。  

 > **power of speech**  
 > After the accident she lost the power of speech.   
 > 那次事故后，她失去了说话能力。  

 > The drug may affect your powers of concentration.  
 > 这种药可能会影响你的注意力。  

### 2.*高义频：* **力量；威力：**  

 > Every storm is an example of the power of nature.   
 > 每场暴风雨都是大自然威力的例证。  

#### 辨析 force, energy, strength, power
四者都有“力”、“力量”之意，但具体意思不同。  

### 3.*高义频：* **控制力；影响力：**  

 > **power over**  
 > Once you are confident about your power over bad situations, problems are just stepping stones to success.  
 > 一旦你对自己掌控恶劣局势的能力感到自信，难题就是你迈向成功的垫脚石。  
 > 来源：2010 广东  

 > He made the mistake of underestimating the power of the press.   
 > 他犯的错误是低估了新闻界的影响力。  

### 4.*高义频：* **统治；政权：**  

 > **in power**  
 > a political party in power   
 > 执政党  

 > **came to power**  
 > The party came to power at the last election.   
 > 这个政党是在上次大选中上台执政的。  

### 5.*高义频：* **权力；职权：**  

 > More than fame or fortune, she wanted power.   
 > 她对权力的渴望甚于名声和财富。  

### 6.*高义频：* **大国；强国：**  

 > an industrial power   
 > 工业大国  

 > **world powers**  
 > world powers   
 > 世界强国  

### 7.*高义频：* **动力；电力；功率：**  

 > **wind / nuclear / solar power**  
 > wind / nuclear / solar power  
 > 风/核/太阳能  

 > **power station**  
 > a power station  
 > 发电站  

 > **power failure / cut**  
 > a power failure / cut  
 > 停电  

 > **engine power**  
 > engine power  
 > 发动机功率

# ***\*practical*** adj
英音 'præktɪkl     美音 'præktɪkl  

| 词频 4 | 口语 1 | 书面 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **(事物) 实际的；实践的：**  

 > The paper seems to me of no practical importance.  
 > 这篇论文在我看来没有什么实际意义。  

 > a teacher with practical experience   
 > 有实践经验的教师  

### 2.*高义频：* **实用的；可实施的**  
反义词 impractical ： 

 > We will listen to your problems and offer you practical advice.  
 > 我们会倾听你的问题，并提供切实可行的建议。  
 > 来源：译林⑤ – 1  

### 3.*高义频：* **(人、想法) 实际的；现实的：**  

 > You must try to be a little more practical.  
 > 你必须努力变得更务实一些。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
When we plan our vacation, mother often offers ________ (practice) suggestions.  
##### 答案 practical  
  

# ***\*practically*** adv
英音 'præktɪkli     美音 'præktɪkli  

| 词频 3 | 口语 1 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **[口语] 几乎；差不多：**  

 > **practically all**  
 > I’ve read practically all of his books.   
 > 我差不多读过他所有的书了。  

### 2.*高义频：* **实际上；事实上：**  

 > It sounds like a good idea, but I don’t think it will work practically.   
 > 这个主意听起来不错，但我认为它实际上行不通。  


# ***\*practice*** n  重难点词汇
英音 'præktɪs     美音 'præktɪs  

| 词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **(反复) 训练；练习：**  

 > **Practice makes perfect**  
 > Practice makes perfect.   
 > 熟能生巧。  

 > John is at baseball practice.   
 > 约翰正在进行棒球训练。  

 > To learn English well requires a lot of practice.   
 > 学好英语需要大量的练习。  

### 2.*高义频：* **实践；实际行动：**  

 > We must combine theory with practice.   
 > 我们必须把理论与实践相结合。  

### 3.*高义频：* **惯例；习惯做法；习俗**  
英译 the usual or expected way of doing sth; a habit or custom：

 > according to the international practice   
 > 按照国际惯例  

 > The practice of students endlessly copying letters and sentences from a blackboard is a thing of the past.   
 > 学生们没完没了地从黑板上抄写单词和句子的做法是过去的事了。  
 > 来源：2012 天津  

 > Customs are common social practices.   
 > 习俗指的是普遍的社会惯常做法。  
 > 来源： 2009 陕西  


固定搭配
---
## \*in practice 
1.**实际上；事实上：**  

 > Your suggestion is very good in theory, but in practice it will not work.   
 > 理论上，你的建议很好，但实际上，是行不通的。  

## \*out of practice 
1.**生疏；疏于练习：**  

 > If you don’t play, you’ll get out of practice.   
 > 不练习就会生疏。  

## \*put ... into practice 
1.**将…付诸实践：**  

 > She’s been able to put a lot of what she’s learnt into practice in her home.  
 > 她在自己家里已经能实践很多自己学到的东西。  
 > 来源：2018 全国  


# ***\*practice*** v
英音 'præktɪs     美音 'præktɪs  

| 词频 4 | 口语 1 | 书面 1 |  

用法点拨  vt & vi

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **实践；练习：**  

 > You’ll never learn to ride a bike if you don’t practise.  
 > 如果不练习，你就永远学不会骑自行车。  

- practice doing sth:

 > You need to practise speaking English to make progress.  
 > 你需要练习讲英语以取得进步。  
 > 来源：外研① – 2  

### 2.*低义频：* **(医生、律师等) 执业；从事 (职业)：**  

 > I intend to practice medicine after graduation.   
 > 我打算毕业后从医。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
As a new driver, I have to practise ________ (park) the car in my small garage again and again.  
##### 来源：2008 上海春改  
##### 答案 parking

# ***\*precise*** adj
英音 prɪ'saɪs     美音 prɪ'saɪs  

| 词频 1 | 书面 1 | 阅读 1 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **精确的；准确的；确切的 (exact)：**  

 > a precise record of events   
 > 对事件的准确记载  

 > It was found at the precise spot where she had left it.  
 > 那件东西正好在她遗落的那个地点找到了。  

### 2.*低义频：* **(人) 细心的；精细的：**  

 > a precise worker   
 > 一丝不苟的工作者

---

 > **know precisely**

 > 很难准确了解这些变化会造成多大影响。

# ***\*predict*** vt
英音 prɪ'dɪkt     美音 prɪ'dɪkt  

| 词频 4 | 书面 1 | 阅读 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **预言；预计 (forecast)：**  

 > predict tomorrow’s weather  
 > 预告明天的天气  

- predict + (that) / wh- 从句：

 > Population experts predict that most people will live in cities in the near future.   
 > 人口专家预言，在不久的将来大多数人都会住到城市里。  
 > 来源：2008 上海春  

 > It’s hard to predict when driverless cars will be everywhere on our roads.  
 > 很难预料何时我们的公路上才会出现大量的无人驾驶汽车。  
 > 来源：2018 北京  

- it is predicted + that 从句：

 > It was predicted that inflation would continue to fall.  
 > 据预测，通货膨胀率将继续下降。  


派生词汇
---
predictable /prɪ'dɪktəbl/ adj   
prediction /prɪ'dɪkʃn/ n [C] & [U]   

真题解析
---
##### 题目  
No matter how carefully you plan your finances, no one can ________ (预测) when the unexpected will happen.   
##### 来源：2014 浙江改  
##### 答案 predict / forecast

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **预言；预报；预告**  


# ***\*prefer*** vt  重难点词汇
英音 prɪ'fɜː(r)     美音 prɪ'fɜːr  

| 词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 |  

用法点拨  (preferred, preferred)

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **更喜欢；更愿意：**  

 > — Tea or coffee?  
 > 喝茶还是咖啡？  

 > — I’d prefer tea, thanks.   
 > 我更喜欢茶，谢谢。  

 > She prefers her coffee black.   
 > 她更喜欢喝清咖啡。  

- prefer sb / sth to do sth:

 > I’d prefer you to start early.   
 > 我更希望你早点出发。  
 > 来源：北师大⑧ – 24  

 > I prefer my English classes to be taught in English only.   
 > 我希望我的英语课是全英语授课。  

- prefer to do sth / doing sth:

 > Some people prefer to do almost everything over the Internet.   
 > 有些人喜欢在网上做几乎一切事情。  
 > 来源： 2013 安徽  

 > I prefer shutting myself in and listening to music all day on Sunday.   
 > 周日我喜欢一整天把自己关在屋里听音乐。  

- prefer (doing) sth to (doing) sth:

 > I prefer the red dress to the green one because it fits me better.   
 > 比起那条绿裙子，我更喜欢那条红色的，因为它更适合我。  
 > 来源：人教① – 3  

 > I would prefer reading books to watching television.  
 > 比起看电视，我还是喜欢读书。  

- prefer + that 从句：

 > They preferred the money (should) be used for building schools and hospitals.   
 > 他们更愿意拿这笔钱来建学校和医院。  

 > I would prefer that you didn’t mention my name.   
 > 我希望你不要提到我的名字。  

Notes: prefer + that 从句结构中，从句中用虚拟语气。  

派生词汇
---
preferred  /prɪ'fəd/ adj   

真题解析
---
##### 题目  
We can eat out if you like, but I would ________ (更喜欢) to stay in.  
##### 来源：2014 陕西  
##### 答案 prefer  
  

# ***\*preference*** n
英音 'prefrəns     美音 'prefrəns  

| 词频 2 | 书面 1 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **偏爱；优先 (权)：**  

 > **preference for**  
 > A teacher should not show preference for any one of his pupils.   
 > 老师不应对任何一个学生有所偏爱。  

 > **in order of preference**  
 > in order of preference   
 > 按优先顺序  

### 2.*高义频：* **偏爱的事物 / 人：**  

 > Wine or beer? Which is your preference?   
 > 葡萄酒还是啤酒？你更喜欢哪种？  


# ***\*prefer…to…*** 


  

英文释义
---
### 1.**喜欢……多于……**  

 > Nowadays, most kids prefer watching TV to reading.  
 > 现在大多数孩子都喜欢看电视而不喜欢阅读。

# ***\*preparation*** n
英音 ˌprepə'reɪʃn     美音 ˌprepə'reɪʃn  

| 词频 3 | 口语 1 | 书面 1 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **准备；预备：**  

 > **preparation for**  
 > I did adequate preparation for the examination.  
 > 我为考试作了充足的准备。  

### 2.*高义频：* **准备工作：**  

 > **preparations for**  
 > All the preparations for the task have been completed, and we’re ready to start.   
 > 这项任务的所有准备工作都已经完成，我们可以开始了。  


固定搭配
---
## \*in preparation for 
1.**为…作准备：**  

 > I want to improve my language skills in preparation for further study overseas.   
 > 我想提高我的语言技能为出国深造作准备。  

## \*make preparations for 
1.**为…作准备：**  

 > They are busy making preparations for the wedding.  
 > 他们正忙着筹备婚礼。  


# ***\*prepare*** v  重难点词汇
英音 prɪ'peə(r)     美音 prɪ'per  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

用法点拨  vt & vi

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **使做好准备；把...准备好**  
英译 to make sth or sb ready to be used or to do sth：

 > prepare dinner  
 > 准备晚餐  

- prepare sth / sb for sb / sth:

 > A hotel room is being prepared for the guest.  
 > 正在为这位客人准备一间旅馆客房。  

 > The function of education is to prepare us for life.  
 > 教育的作用是让我们对生活有所准备。  
 > 来源：2011 安徽  

### 2.*高义频：* **(使自己) 有准备**  
英译 to make yourself ready to do sth or for sth that you expect to happen：

- prepare for sth:

 > Hope for the best, and prepare for the worst.  
 > 抱最好的希望，做最坏的打算。  

 > The lectures help students prepare for college mathematics.  
 > 这些课程有助于学生为大学数学做好准备。  
 > 来源：2012 北京改  

- prepare oneself (for sth):

 > I closed my eyes and prepared myself for his burst of anger.  
 > 我闭上眼睛做好了准备，等他大发雷霆。  
 > 来源：2013 陕西  

- prepare (oneself) to do sth:

 > Buy the album, and prepare to be amazed.  
 > 买下这张专辑，准备好感受惊喜吧。  

 > The troops prepared themselves to go into battle.  
 > 部队准备开赴战场。  


# ***\*prepared*** adj
英音 prɪ'peəd     美音 prɪ'perd  

| 词频 4 | 口语 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **准备好的；有所准备的：**  
反义词 unprepared 

 > Our monitor presented our teacher with the prepared flowers.  
 > 我们班长给老师献上了准备好的花。  
 > 来源：2012 陕西书面表达  

 > **well prepared**  
 > It seems you’re well prepared.   
 > 看来你做好了充分的准备。  
 > 来源：2008 重庆  

- be / get prepared for:

 > We should improve our study methods and get well prepared for examinations.   
 > 我们应该改进学习方法，为考试做好充分准备。  

- be / get prepared to do sth:

 > **be fully prepared to**  
 > All the competitors must be fully prepared to give the best performance.  
 > 所有参赛者一定要做好充分准备，以便发挥最佳水平。  
 > 来源：2009 天津书面表达改

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **颁发；授予；赠送**  
英译 to give sth to sb, especially formally at a ceremony：

 > The Grammy Awards are presented every year in the music industry in the United States.   
 > 格莱美奖在美国音乐界每年颁奖一次。  
 > 来源： 外研⑥ – 4  

- present sth to sb / present sb with sth:

 > The young man presented the water to the old man. / The young man presented the old man with the water.  
 > 年轻人把水给老人端上来。  
 > 来源：2010 广东  

### 2.*高义频：* **提出；呈递**  
英译 to show or offer sth for other people to look at or consider：

 > **presented,to**  
 > We presented three options to the Students’ Union for discussion.  
 > 我们向学生会提出了三种选择以供讨论。  

 > At the end of the programme, the students presented papers on their research.   
 > 项目结束时，学生提交了他们的研究论文。  

### 3.*高义频：* **呈现**  
英译 to show or describe sth / sb in a particular way：

 > Classic works, written by masters, present great thoughts through fascinating stories and language.  
 > 大师们所著的经典作品，通过极具吸引力的故事和语言呈现出伟大的思想。  
 > 来源：2014 浙江书面表达  

### 4.*低义频：* **招致；带来：**  

 > The EXIT signs could not be seen clearly, which presented potential safety issues.  
 > “出口”指示牌看不清楚会带来安全隐患。  

 > **present,problems**  
 > Large classes present great problems to many teachers.  
 > 大班教学给许多老师造成很大的困难。  

### 5.*低义频：* **上演；推出**  

 > The theater company presents a new production of King Lear,  
 > 剧团推出全新制作的《李尔王》。  


派生词汇
---
presenter /prɪ'zentə(r)/ n [C]  

# ***\*present*** n  重难点词汇
英音 'preznt     美音 'preznt  

| 词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 1 |  

用法点拨  [常用the present]

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **目前；现在：**  

 > I’ve decided to live in the present and not spend my life regretting the past or dreading the future.  
 > 我决定活在当下，不再浪费生命悔恨过去或担忧未来。  


固定搭配
---
## \*at present
1.**现在；目前：**  

 > My classmate is at present in hospital with a broken leg.   
 > 我的同学因为摔断了腿目前正在住院。  
 > 来源：2009 陕西改  

## \*for the present 
1.**暂时 (for the moment)：**  

 > We shall not need any more for the present.   
 > 我们暂时不需要更多的了。  

 > I can’t remember it for the present.   
 > 我一时想不起来了。  


# ***\*present*** adj  重难点词汇
英音 'preznt     美音 'preznt  

| 词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **现在的；如今的：**  

 > **the present,situation**  
 > the present difficulties / problems / situation   
 > 当前的困难/问题/形势  

 > **At the present time**  
 > At the present time we have no explanation for this.  
 > 目前我们对此不作任何解释。  

### 2.*高义频：* **在场的；出席的：**  

 > **present at**  
 > All students are required to be present at the school meeting.  
 > 所有学生务必出席全校大会。  

 > Everybody present welcomed the decision.   
 > 在场的所有人都对这个决定表示欢迎。  


派生词汇
---
presently /'prezntli/ adv

# ***\*press*** v
英音 pres     美音 pres  

| 词频 4 | 口语 3 | 书面 2 |  

用法点拨  vt & vi

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **压 (push)；按；挤；推：**  

 > **press a button / switch**  
 > press a button / switch  
 > 按下按钮 / 开关  

 > She pressed her face against the window.   
 > 她把脸贴在窗上。  

 > She pressed down hard on the gas pedal and the car leapt forwards.   
 > 她猛踩油门，车向前冲去。  

### 2.*低义频：* **催促；逼迫 (push / urge)：**  

 > Pressed by my friends and relations, I decided to seize the opportunity.   
 > 在朋友和家人的催促下，我决定抓住机会。  
 > 来源：人教⑧ – 3  


固定搭配
---
## \*press on 
1.**(不顾困难) 继续进行：**  

 > He pressed on and finally got passed the finishing line.  
 > 他继续前进，最终冲过了终点线。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
He ________ (按下) the button and the doorbell rang.   
##### 来源：2009 全国  
##### 答案 pressed / pushed

英音 pres     美音 pres  

| 词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 |  

用法点拨  [C]

英文释义
---
### 1.*低义频：* **按；压；推；挤：**  

 > Give it a press.   
 > 按一下它。  

### 2.*高义频：* **出版社；印刷厂：**  

 > the Oxford University Press   
 > 牛津大学出版社  

### 3.*高义频：* **报刊新闻业；新闻界：**  

 > **local press**  
 > the local press   
 > 当地报刊  

 > **freedom of the press**  
 > the freedom of the press   
 > 新闻自由  


# ***\*pressure*** n
英音 'preʃə(r)     美音 'preʃər  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **挤压；(物理学) 压力；压强：**  

 > **air / blood pressure**  
 > air / blood pressure   
 > 气/血压  

 > The nurse applied pressure to his arm to stop the bleeding.   
 > 护士用力按住他的手臂来止血。  

### 2.*高义频：* **(精神上的，外界施加的) 压力：**  

 > **under pressure**  
 > Some people work better under pressure.   
 > 有些人在有压力时工作表现会更好。  

 > **put,pressure on**  
 > I know studying is very important, but my parents put too much pressure on me.   
 > 我知道学习很重要，但父母给我施加了太多的压力。  
 > 来源：2008 浙江  

 > pressures of life  
 > 生活压力  


# ***\*pretend*** v
英音 prɪ'tend     美音 prɪ'tend  

| 词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 1 |  

用法点拨  vt & vi

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **假装；装作：**  

 > What’s the good of pretending?   
 > 装假有什么用呢？  

- pretend to do sth:

 > When his mother came in, he pretended to be doing his homework.   
 > 妈妈进来时，他假装在做作业。  

- pretend (to sb) + that 从句:

 > He pretended to his family that everything was fine.  
 > 他对家人假装一切都好。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
Miss Harper closed her eyes and ________ to be asleep.   
##### 来源：2010 陕西  
##### 答案 pretended

| 词频 4 | 口语 3 | 书面 1 |  

英文释义
---

 > Pollution prevents people from seeing objects in the sky that they could see quite easily in the past.

# ***\*previous*** adj
英音 'priːviəs     美音 'priːviəs  

| 词频 3 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **以前的；先前的：**  

 > **the previous chapter**  
 > in the previous chapter   
 > 在上一章中  

 > He has no previous experience of this kind of work.  
 > 他以前没有做这类工作的经验。  


固定搭配
---
## \*previous to 
1.**[正式用语] 在…之前：**  

 > Previous to this, scientific experiments did not show a definite link between mobile phone use and cancer.  
 > 在这之前，科学实验没有表明在使用手机和患癌症之间存在明确的关联。  
 > 来源：译林⑦ – 1  


派生词汇
---

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **价格；价钱：**  

 > **high / low price**  
 > at a high / low price   
 > 以高/低价  

### 2.*高义频：* **代价；牺牲：**  

 > **paid a,price**  
 > We paid a heavy price for the victory.   
 > 我们为胜利付出了沉重的代价。  


固定搭配
---
## \*at the price of 
1.**以…的代价：**  

 > She achieved success at the price of her health.  
 > 她的成功是以牺牲自身健康为代价的。

 > **are priced at**  
 > The tickets are priced at $10 each.   
 > 门票价格为每张10美元。

# ***\*pride*** n
英音 praɪd     美音 praɪd  

| 词频 4 | 口语 1 | 书面 1 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **自豪；骄傲：**  

 > **a sense of,pride**  
 > a sense of national pride  
 > 民族自豪感  

 > I was filled with pride.   
 > 我满怀自豪。  

### 2.*高义频：* **引起自豪的人 / 事物：**  

 > **the pride of**  
 > I think he is the pride of our Chinese people.  
 > 我认为他是我们中国人的骄傲。  
 > 来源：北师大⑥ – 16  

 > sb’s pride and joy  
 > 使某人感到骄傲和快乐的人 / 事物  

### 3.*高义频：* **自尊；尊严：**  

 > His pride prevents him from doing anything dishonourable.  
 > 他的自尊使他不会做出任何不光彩的事情。  

### 4.*高义频：* **自负；傲慢：**  

 > Pride goes before a fall.  
 > 骄兵必败。  


固定搭配
---
## \*take pride in 
1.**对…感到自豪：**  

 > People tend to take pride in keeping everything in their street fresh.  
 > 人们往往会为保持自己的街道清爽而感到自豪。  
 > 来源：2018 浙江  

## \*with pride 
1.**自豪地：**  

 > I looked with pride at what I had achieved.   
 > 回顾过去的成就，我感到很自豪。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
Rebecca was the ________ (骄傲) of her family.  
##### 来源：2012 全国  
##### 答案 pride

# ***\*principal*** n
英音 'prɪnsəpl     美音 'prɪnsəpl  

| 词频 1 | 阅读 1 |  

用法点拨  [C]

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **校长 (headteacher)**  


# ***\*principle*** n
英音 'prɪnsəpl     美音 'prɪnsəpl  

| 词频 3 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 1 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **原理；原则**  
英译 the basic idea that a plan or system is based on：

 > **basic principle**  
 > the basic principle  
 > 基本原理/基本原则  

 > **guiding principle**  
 > Excellent customer service should be our guiding principle.   
 > 优秀的客户服务应该成为我们的指导原则。  

### 2.*高义频：* **道德准则；行为准则**  
英译 a moral rule or belief about what is right and wrong, that influences how you behave：

 > **man of principle**  
 > a man of principle  
 > 有原则的人  

 > **it’s against my principles**  
 > I refuse to lie about it; it’s against my principles.   
 > 我绝不为此事撒谎，那有悖我的原则。  

 > **on principle**  
 > She’d never ask to borrow money, on principle.   
 > 原则上，她从不向别人借钱。  

### 3.*高义频：* **(机器等的) 工作原理；(自然界的) 定律；法则**  
英译 a general or scientific law that explains how sth works or why sth happens：

 > Archimedes’ principle   
 > 阿基米德定律  

 > These machines both work on the same principle.   
 > 这两台机器的工作原理是相同的。  


固定搭配
---
## \*in principle
1.*高义频：* **理论上；原则上：**  

 > I agree with it in principle but I doubt if it will happen in practice.   
 > 理论上我同意，但是不知道实际上能否可行。  

2.*高义频：* **大体上；基本上：**  

 > We agree with it in principle but we still need to discuss the details.  
 > 我们大体上同意，但是仍需讨论细节。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
Anyway, I can’t cheat him — it’s against all my ________ (原则).   
##### 来源：2011 浙江改  
##### 答案 principles  
  

# ***\*print*** v
英音 prɪnt     美音 prɪnt  

| 词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 1 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **打印；印刷：**  

 > print the document   
 > 打印文件  

 > Six thousand copies of the book are printed.  
 > 这本书印了6 000册。  

### 2.*高义频：* **刊登 (publish)：**  

 > It is his wish that his stories would be printed in local newspapers.   
 > 他希望自己的故事会刊登在当地报纸上。

用法点拨  [C]

英文释义

 > **health / family problems**  
 > health / family problems  
 > 健康 / 家庭问题  

 > **cause / solve a problem**  
 > cause / solve a problem  
 > 引起 / 解决问题  

 > **I’ve been having problems with**  
 > I’ve been having problems with my computer system.  
 > 我的电脑系统一直有问题。  
 > 来源：2010 北京改  

### 2.*低义频：* **(考试、教科书中的) 问题：**  

 > She set her pupils many mathematical problems.   
 > 她给学生们布置了很多数学题。  


固定搭配
---
## \*no problem
1.*高义频：* **[表示乐于相助或事情容易做]没问题：**  

 > — How about meeting at the nearby restaurant?   
 > 在附近的餐馆见面如何？  

 > — No problem.   
 > 没问题。  

2.*高义频：* **没关系；不客气：**  

 > — Thanks for the ride.   
 > 谢谢你载我一程。  

 > — No problem.   
 > 不客气。  

#### 辨析 problem, question
二者都可译作“问题”。  


真题解析
---
##### 题目  
— Are you sure you’re ready for the test?
— ________ (没问题). I’m well prepared for it.
  
##### 来源：2016 浙江改  
##### 答案 No problem

Studies have shown that the right and left ear _______ sound differently.

# ***\*produce*** vt
英音 prə'djuːs     美音 prə'duːs  

| 词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **产生；引起**  
英译 to cause a particular result or effect (bring about)：

 > Giving sometimes produces nice results.  
 > 给予有时会产生好的结果。  
 > 来源：2013 陕西  

 > Childhood experiences produce far-reaching effect on the health of grown-ups.  
 > 儿时的经历对成年后的健康会产生深远的影响。  

### 2.*高义频：* **生产；创作**  
英译 to make, write etc. sth to be bought, used or enjoyed by people：

 > **mass-produce**  
 > In 1914 Henry Ford began to mass-produce cars using assembly lines.  
 > 1914年亨利·福特开始使用流水线大量生产汽车。  

 > **produce,from**  
 > Each year, world-famous artists are invited to design and produce works of art from the ice.  
 > 每年，一些世界闻名的艺术家都被邀请来用冰块设计和创作艺术作品。  
 > 来源：2010 全国  

### 3.*高义频：* **出产；生育：**  

 > Australia has produced some famous painters and world-class writers.  
 > 澳大利亚出了一些著名画家和世界级的作家。  
 > 来源：北师大④ – 12  

 > He had a cow which produced milk every day.  
 > 他有一头奶牛，每天都产奶。  
 > 来源：2015 广东改  

### 4.*低义频：* **监制；制作 (电影、戏剧等)：**  

 > In the last few years thousands of films have been produced all over the world.  
 > 过去几年中，全世界制作了数千部电影。  
 > 来源：2011 天津

# ***\*promise*** n  重难点词汇
英音 'prɒmɪs     美音 'prɑːmɪs  

| 词频 5 | 口语 1 | 书面 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **诺言；许诺；承诺：**  

 > **promise to**  
 > his promise to his father  
 > 他对父亲的承诺  

 > **break / make a / one’s promise**  
 > break / make a / one’s promise  
 > 违背诺言 / 作出承诺  

 > carry out one’s promise   
 > 履行诺言  

 > **keep,a promise**  
 > keep / live up to a promise  
 > 信守诺言  

- promise to do sth:

 > Don’t forget your promise to visit me next week.   
 > 别忘了你答应下周来看我。  

- promise + (that) 从句:

 > Give me your promise that you’ll never be late again.   
 > 答应我你绝不再迟到了。  

### 2.*高义频：* **(有) 指望；(有) 前途：**  

 > **shows,promise**  
 > Her work shows great promise.   
 > 她的工作很有前途。  


真题解析
---

The young man made a promise ________ his parents that he would try to earn his own living after graduation.  
##### 来源：2008 湖北改  
##### 答案 to  
  

# ***\*promise*** v  重难点词汇
英音 'prɒmɪs     美音 'prɑːmɪs  

| 词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **许诺；保证；答应：**  

 > — She’s not coming tonight.   
 > 她今晚不来了。  

 > — But she promised.   
 > 但她答应过的。  

- promise to do sth:

 > The new monitor promised to do the best she could for us all.  
 > 新班长承诺会为我们大家竭尽全力。  

- promise (sb) + (that) 从句:

 > I promise that you will get all your money back.   
 > 我保证你会拿回你所有的钱。  
 > 来源：北师大⑧ – 23  

- promise sb sth / promise sth to sb:

 > She has been promised a new bike.   
 > 有人答应给她买辆新自行车。  

 > I’ve promised the book to Susan.   
 > 我已经答应把这本书给苏珊了。  

### 2.*低义频：* **有...的希望；有...的可能：**  

 > Those clouds promise rain tomorrow.   
 > 那些云预示着明天有可能下雨。  

- promise to be sth:

 > It promises to be a fine day.   
 > 天气有望好转。  


派生词汇
---
promising /'prɒmɪsɪŋ/ adj   
 > a promising lawyer  
 > 有前途的律师

---

##### 答案 to be

# ***\*protect*** v
英音 prə'tekt     美音 prə'tekt  

| 词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 |  

英文释义
---
### 1.*高义频：* **vt & vi 保护；防护：**  

 > protect the earth  
 > 保护地球  

- protect sb / sth from sth:

 > We put a sheet of plastic across the floor to protect us from the damp.  
 > 我们在地板上铺了一块塑料膜以防潮。  
 > 来源：2009 四川  

 > Something must be done to protect the environment from being polluted.  
 > 必须采取措施以保护环境免受污染。  

- protect (sb / sth) against sth:

 > Physical exercise can protect you against heart disease.  
 > 体育锻炼可以预防心脏病。  

 > Waxing your car will help protect against rust.  
 > 给车打蜡可以防止生锈。  

#### 辨析 defend, guard, protect
1. 三者都含有“保护”之意。  


派生词汇
---

 > **protective of**  
 > He’s very protective of his younger brother.  
 > 他很爱护他的弟弟。

---

##### 来源：2006 陕西  
##### 答案 protect
